RIG VEDA - MODERN ENGLISH & HINGLISH REWRITE

==================================================
RIG-VEDA, BOOK 9
==================================================

--------------------------------------------------
HYMN I. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09001.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Purely flowing, O Soma, in a sweet stream,
press for Indra, for his libation.
2. Queller of foes, friend to all, he has reached his place,
his iron home, his heavenly abode.
3. Be the best slayer of Vṛtra, the best giver of joy,
promote the wealth of our princes' offerings.
4. Flow forward with your juice to the gods' feast,
flow here for our strength and renown.
5. O Indu, we come to you each day, with one purpose only:
to you alone do we pray.
6. With this eternal fleece may Sūrya's Daughter cleanse
your foaming Soma.
7. Ten slender maidens grasp him in the press,
hold him tight on the final day.
8. The virgins send him forth; they play the skin musician,
blowing the triple foe-repelling meath.
9. Around him blend unbroken cows, for Indra's drink,
the fresh Soma with their milk.
10. In this wild ecstasy, Indra slays all Vṛtras:
the Hero pours his wealth upon us.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN II. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09002.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Soma, flow on, inviting Gods, speed to the purifying cloth:
   Enter Indra, as a Bull.
   
2. As mighty food speed hitherward, Indu, as a most splendid Steer:
   Sit in thy place as one with strength.
   
3. The well-loved meath was made to flow, the stream of the creative juice
   by the Sage drew waters to himself.
   
4. The mighty waters, yea, the floods accompany thee Mighty One,
   When thou wilt clothe thee with the milk.
   
5. The lake is brightened in the floods. Soma, our Friend, heaven's prop and stay,
   Falls on the purifying cloth.
   
6. The tawny Bull hath bellowed, fair as mighty Mitra to behold:
   He shines together with the Sun.
   
7. Songs, Indu, active in their might are beautified for thee, wherewith
   Thou deckest thee for our delight.
   
8. To thee who givest ample room we pray, to win the joyous draught:
   Great are the praise& due to thee.
   
9. Indu as, Indra's Friend, on us pour with a stream of sweetness, like
   Parjanya sender of the rain.
   
10 Winner of kine, Indu, art thou, winner of heroes, steeds, and strength
   Primeval Soul of sacrifice.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN III. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09003.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Here, the Immortal God soars like a bird on its wings,
To settle in the wooden vats.
2. This God, prepared with song, races swiftly through winding paths,
Invincible as he flows.
3. As he flows, this God adorns himself, like a warhorse for men,
Devout and skilled in holy songs.
4. Like a warrior leading heroes, as he flows, he seeks
All precious gifts to win.
5. As he flows, this God rides like a chariot, giving gifts;
He lets his voice be heard by all.
6. Praised by the sacred bards, this God dives into waters,
Bestowing rich gifts on the worshipper.
7. With his stream, he rushes across regions, into heaven,
Roaring as he flows.
8. Flowing for sacrifice, he ascends to heaven across regions,
Unyielding, unstoppable.
9. After the path of old times, this God, pressed out for Deities,
Flows tawny to the cloth.
10. This Lord of many Holy Laws, even at birth generating strength,
Effuses, flowing in a stream.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN IV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09004.htm
--------------------------------------------------
O Soma, flow on your path and win glory high,
And make us better than we are.

Win the light, win heavenly light, and all felicities,
And make us better than we are.

Win skill and mental might, O Soma, drive back our enemies,
And make us better than we are.

Ye purifiers, purify Soma for Indra, for his drink:
Make us better than we are.

Give us our share in the Sun by your mental power and aids,
And make us better than we are.

Through your mental power and aid, let us see the Sun long,
Make us better than we are.

Well-armed Soma, pour a stream of double wealth to us,
And make us better than we are.

As one victorious, unyielding in battle, pour forth wealth to us,
And make us better than we are.

By worship, Pavamana! Let men strengthen you to uphold the Law,
Make us better than we are.

O Indu, bring us wealth in horses, manifold, quickening all life,
And make us better than we are.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN V Āprīs.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09005.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. ENKINDLED, Pavamana, Lord, sends forth his light everywhere
 In a friendly way, the bellowing Bull.
 2 He, Pavamana, Self-produced, strides forward sharpening his horns:
 He shines through the sky.
 3 Bright as wealth, adorable, with brilliance Pavamana shines,
 Mighty with the streams of meath.
 4 The tawny Pavamana, who long ago spread grass with might,
 Is worshiped, God among the Gods.
 5 The golden, the Celestial Doors are raised high by their frames,
 By Pavamana glorified.
 6 With passion Pavamana yearns for the great lofty pair, well-formed
 Like beautiful maidens, Night and Dawn.
 7 Both Gods who watch over men I call, Celestial Herald: Indra’s Self
 Is Pavamana, indeed, the Bull.
 8 This, Pavamana’s sacrifice, will the three beauteous Goddesses,
 Sarasvati and Bharati and Iḷā, Mighty One, attend.
 9 I summon Tvaṣṭar hither, our protector, champion, firstborn,
 Indu is Indra, tawny Steer; Pavamana is Prajāpati.
 10 O Pavamana, with the meath in streams anoint Vanaspati,
 The ever-green, golden-hooded, refulgent, with a thousand branches.
 11 Come to the consecrating rite of Pavamana, all ye Gods—
 Vāyu, Sūrya, Bṛhaspati, Indra, and Agni, in harmony.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN VI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09006.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Soma, flow on with a pleasant stream, a devoted Bull to the Gods,
Our friend, to the woollen sieve.
2. Pour hitherward, as Indra’s Self, Indu, that gladdening stream of thine,
And send us coursers full of strength.
3. Flow to the filter hitherward, pouring that ancient gladdening juice,
Streaming forth power and high renown.
4. Hither the sparkling drops have flowed, like waters down a steep descent,
They have reached Indra purified.
5. Whom, having passed the filter, ten dames cleanse, as ’twere a vigorous steed,
While he disports himself in the wood—
6. The strong-juice steer pours forth milk for feast and service of the Gods,
For him who bears away the draught.
7. Effused, the God flows onward with his stream to Indra, to the God,
So that his milk may strengthen him.
8. Soul of the sacrifice, the juice effused flows quickly on: he keeps
His ancient wisdom of a Sage.
9. So pouring forth, as Indra’s Friend, strong drink, best Gladdener! for the feast,
Thou, even in secret, storest hymns.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN VII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09007.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The glorious drops flow forth for the maintenance of Law,
Knowing this sacrifice’s path.

2. In the mighty waters, the stream of mead sinks, most excellent,
The best offering of all in worth.

3. Around the holy place, the Steer true, guileless, noblest, sends out
Continuous voices in the wood.

4. When clad in manly strength, the Sage flows in celestial wisdom round,
The Strong wins the light of heaven.

5. When purified, he sits as King above the hosts, among his folk,
When the sages bring him near.

6. Dear, golden-colored, in the fleece he sinks and settles in the wood:
The Singer shows his zeal in hymns.

7. He goes to Indra, Vāyu, to the Aśvins, as his custom is,
With sweet juice that gives them joy.

8. The streams of pleasant Soma flow to Bhaga, Mitra-Varuṇa—
Well-known through his mighty powers.
Heaven and Earth, riches of mead to win us wealth:
Grant us treasures and renown.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN VIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09008.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Following Indra’s wish, these Soma juices have flowed,
Boosting his mighty power.

2. Placed in the bowl, pure and flowing, to Vāyu and the Aśvins,
May they grant us great heroic strength.

3. Soma, as you are purified, stir up Indra’s heart,
So that he sits in sacrifice’s place.

4. With your ten swift fingers adorned, seven ministers urge you on:
The sages have rejoiced in you.

5. When through the filter you are poured, clothe yourself with a milk robe,
To be a joyful draught for the gods.

6. Within the jars, when you are purified, Soma, bright red and golden,
You wear a milk robe.

7. Flow onto us and make us rich. Drive all our enemies away.
O Indu, flow into your friend.

Send down the rain from heaven, a stream of prosperity from earth.
Give us, O Soma, victory in war.

9. May we obtain you, Indra’s drink, who see men and find light,
Gain you, and offspring and sustenance.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN IX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09009.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The Heavenly Sage whose heart is wise, when placed between both hands and pressed,
 Sends us delightful powers of life.
2. Onward, onward to a glorious home; dear to the people without deceit,
 With excellent enjoyment, flow.
3. He, the bright Son, when born enlightened his Parents who had risen,
 Great Son, great Lawgivers.
4. Urged by the seven devotions, he stirred the guileless rivers that
 Have magnified the Single Eye.
5. These helped the Youthful One, supreme over all, invincible,
 Even Indu, Indra! In your law.
6. The immortal Courser, good to draw, looks down upon the Seven: the source
 Has satisfied the Goddesses.
7. Help us in holy rites, O Man: O Pavamana, drive away
 Dark shadows that must be faced in battle.
8. Make the paths ready for a newer hymn evermore:
 Make the lights shine as they once did.
9. Give, Pavamana, high renown, give kine and steeds and hero sons:
 Win for us wisdom, win the light.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN X. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09010.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. LIKE race cars roaring forward, like horses eager for fame,
 Have Soma drops flowed forth for wealth.
 2 Forth have they rushed from clasped hands, like racing chariots urged to speed,
 Like joyful songs of singing men.
 3 The Somas adorn themselves with milk, like kings adorned with praise,
 And with seven priests, the sacrifice.
 4 Pressed for the sweet draught, the drops flow forth abundantly with song,
 The Soma juices in a stream.
 5 Winning Vivasvan’s glory and producing Dawn’s light, the Suns
 Pass through the openings of the cloth.
 6 The singing men of olden times open the doors of sacred songs—
 Men, for the mighty to receive.
 7 Combined in close fellowship sit the seven priests, the brotherhood,
 Filling the place of the One.
 8 He grants us kinship with the gods, and with the Sun unites our gaze:
 The Sage’s offspring has appeared.
 9 The Sun with his dear eye beholds that quarter of the sky which priests
 Have placed within the sacred cell.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XL Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09011.htm
--------------------------------------------------
Sing forth to Indu, oh men, to the pure one we offer worship.
Together with your sweet nectar, the Atharvans have mixed milk,
Divine, dedicated to the Devas.
Bring, by your flow, prosperity to cattle, to the people, to horses.
Prosperity, O King, to the growth of plants.

Praise Soma, brown in hue, of great might.
The Red One reaching up to the heavens.
Purify Soma as it is poured, with stones that swiftly move,
And pour the sweet milk into the meath.

With humble reverence, bring near; mix the libation with the curds:
Offer Indu to Indu, to Indra.

Soma, the chief who overcomes foes, fulfilling the will,
Bestow prosperity on our cattle.
Heart-knower, Sovereign of the heart, you are infused, O Soma,
That Indra may drink you and be joyful.

O Soma Pavamana, grant us wealth and heroic strength—
Indu! With Indra as ally.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09012.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Pour the Soma drops to Indra, rich and sweet, in sacrifice.
2. Like mother cows to their calves, the sages call out to Indra,
Calling him to drink the Soma juice.
3. In the stream’s wave, Soma dwells, distilling joy, in his seat,
Resting on a wild cow’s hide.
4. Far-sighted Soma, Sage and Seer, worshipped at the heart of heaven,
In the center of the straining cloth of wool.
5. Indu holds Soma close within the jars, on the purifying sieve.
6. Indu sends a voice high up to the realms of the air,
Shaking the vase that drops with mead.
7. The Tree that sings its praises without end yields heavenly milk
Among our hymns, urging generations on.
8. The Wise One, with the Sage’s stream, urged by Soma to move on,
To the dear places in the sky.
9. O Pavamana, grant us wealth bright with a thousand lights, yes.
O Indu, give us swift aid.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09013.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Passed through, the Soma flows in thousand streams, purified, to Indra’s special place.
2. Sing forth, you men who seek help, to Pavamana, to the Sage,
Pour it out to entertain the Gods.
3. Thousand-power drops of Soma are purified for victory,
Hymned to become the Gods’ feast.
4. Bring us abundant food, Indu, to win the spoil,
With splendid manly might.
5. May they give us wealth in thousands and heroic power—
These Godlike Soma drops, effused.
6. Like horses urged by their drivers, they are poured forth for victory,
Swiftly through the woollen straining-cloth.
7. Noisily flow the Soma drops, like milch-kine to their calves:
They run forth from both the hands.
8. As the Gladdener loved by Indra, O Pavamana, with a roar
Drive all our enemies away.
9. O Pavamamas, driving off the godless, looking on the light,
Sit in the place of sacrifice.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XIV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09014.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. THE SEER WASHES AROUND THE RIVER, CARRYING A LOVED HYMN.
 2 WHEN THE FIVE KINDRED GROUPS, ACTIVELY DUTIFUL, WITH THE SONG
 INSTALL HIM, THE POWERFUL ONE,
 3 THEN IN HIS MILK THAT IS STRONG, ALL THE GODS ARE JOYFUL,
 WHEN HE WEARIES HIM IN MILK.
 4 FREE FROM HIS BODILY PARTS, LEAVING HIS SEPARATED MEMBERS,
 HE MEETS HIS OWN COMPANION HERE.
 5 BY THE DAUGHTERS OF THE PRIEST, LIKE A BEAUTIFUL YOUTH, HE IS ADORNED,
 MAKING THE MILK, AS IT WERE, HIS ROBE.
 6 OVER THE SLIPPERY FINGERS, DESIRING MILK, IN A CURVE HE GOES,
 AND SPEAKS THE VOICE HE HAS FOUND.
 7 THE QUICK FINGERS APPROACH, ADORNING THE LORD OF STRENGTH:
 THEY GRASP THE STRONG HORSE'S BACK.
 8 COMPREHENDING ALL THE TREASURES THAT ARE IN THE HEAVENS AND ON EARTH,
 COME, SOMA, OUR FAITHFUL FRIEND.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09015.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. WITH the skilled hands, through the song, this Hero swiftly arrives at Indra’s place.
2. IN holy thoughts, he deeply considers the great worship of the gods.
3. LIKE a well-trained horse, he is led out, as the gleaming paths are trodden by swift horses.
4. HE raises his horns high, the Bull leading the herd, performing heroic deeds with might.
5. HE rides, a vigorous steed, adorned with radiant golden rays, becoming the sovereign of the rivers.
6. HE descends into the reservoirs, bringing rich treasures close together.
7. MEN adorn him in the vats, worthy to be adorned, he who brings abundant food.
8. HIM, TEN fingers and SEVEN songs make beautiful, well-equipped, the best of cheerers.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XVI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09016.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The pressers pour out your nectar for rapturous joy,  
The sweet sap flows like a flood.

2. With strength we sift through the sieve him who brings might and wins the kine,  
Enveloped in water with his juice.

3. Pour on the sieve the Soma, never subdued in waters, waterless,  
And make it pure for Indra’s drink.

4. Moved by the purifier’s thought, the Soma flows into the sieve:  
By wisdom it has found its home.

5. Indra, with humble homage, have the Soma drops flowed forth to you,  
Contending for the glorious prize.

6. Purified in his fleecy garb, attaining every beauty, he  
Stands, hero-like, amid the kine.

7. Swelling, as if to heights of heaven, the stream of the creative juice  
Falls lightly on the cleansing sieve.

8. Thus, Soma, purifying him who knows song among the living men,  
Thou wanderest through the cloth of wool.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XVII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09017.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. LIKE rivers rushing down a steep incline, slaying the Vṛtras, full of zeal,
 The swift Soma-streams have flowed.
2. The drops of Soma juice fall like rain upon the earth:
 To Indra flow the Soma-streams.
3. With swelling waves, the joy-bringing drink, the Soma, flows into the sieve,
 Liking the gods and slaying demons.
4. It rushes to the pitchers, poured into the sieve it grows strong
 At sacrifices through the lauds.
5. Soma, you shine, rising up to heaven as if above light’s triple realm,
 Moving swiftly to hasten the Sun.
6. To him, the leader of sacrifice, singers and bards have sung their songs,
 Offering what he loves to see.
7. The men, the sages with their hymns, eager for help, deck you strong and steady,
 Deck you for service of the gods.
8. Flow onward to the stream of mead, efficacious in your home,
 Fair, to be drunk at sacrifice.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XVIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09018.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Soma, you dwell on the hills, flowing into the sieve:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.
 2 You are a sacred bard, a sage; the mead is the offering of your sap:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.
 3 All deities come together in harmony to drink from you:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.
 4 He who holds all the many desired treasures in his hands:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.
 5 He who milks out this mighty pair, the Earth and Heaven, like mother cows:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.
 6 He who flows mightily around these two halves of the world:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.
 7 The Strong One, purified, cries aloud in the pitchers:
 You are all-bountiful in your feast.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XIX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09019.htm
--------------------------------------------------
O Soma, purify yourself and bring us the wondrous treasure, meet
For lauds, that is in earth and heaven.

For you two, Indra and Soma, are Lords of the light, Lords of the kine:
Great Rulers, may your songs prosper.

The tawny Steer, while cleansed among the living, bellowing on the grass,
Has sunk and settled in his home.

Over the Steer’s productive flow the sacred songs resound,
Mothers of the darling Son.

Has he not, purified and impregnated, filled the kine that long to meet their Lord,
The kine that yield the shining milk?

Bring near us those who stand aloof and strike fear into our enemies:
O Pavamana, grant us wealth.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XX Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09020.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The Sage flows forth through the fine cloth to the feast of the gods,
Subduing all our foes.
2. For he, as Pavamana, brings innumerable wealth in the form of cattle
To the singers.
3. You grasp all things with your mind, and purify yourself with thoughts,
O Soma, grant us renown.
4. Pour high glory upon us, send sure riches to our generous lords,
Bring sustenance to those who sing your praise.
5. As you are cleansed, O Wonder Horse, O Soma, you have entered, like
A righteous king, into the songs.
6. Like a swift horse in the flood, made clean by hands, you rest in the jars.
7. Playing like a generous chief, you go, Soma, to the sieve,
Lending the laud a hero’s strength.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09021.htm
--------------------------------------------------
To Indra pour these flowing drops, these Soma spirits lively.
Exhilarating, finding light;
Driving off enemies, making space for the sacrificer, willingly
Bringing their praise vital force.
Lightly dancing them, the drops flow to one common pool,
And fall into the river’s wave.
These Pavamanas have earned great blessings, like horses yoked to a chariot;
With regard to us, O Soma drops, grant your manifold desire
To him who has given us nothing yet.
Bring us our wish with this intent, as a craftsman brings a new wheel:
Flow pure and shining with the stream.
These drops have shouted with a loud voice: like swift horses they ran the course,
And stirred the good man’s song to life.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09022.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. These quick Soma streams stir themselves like swift horses,
Like chariots, like armies hurrying forth.
2. They move swiftly, as wide winds do, like storms of Parjanya's rain,
And like the flickering flames of fire.
3. These Soma juices, blended with curds, pure and skilled in sacred songs,
Have won by song their heart's desire.
4. Immortal, cleansed, since first they flowed, they never tire,
To reach the realms and their paths.
5. They travel over the peaks of earth and sky,
And this is the highest realm of all.
6. They reach the highest thread spun out,
And this is deemed the most high.
7. You, Soma, rich in cattle you've seized from stingy owners,
You called forth the spun-out thread.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09023.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Swift Soma drops have flowed in streams of mead, the joyous drink,
 For all kinds of sacred knowledge.
2. Hither to a new resting-place the ancient Living Ones have come.
 They made the Sun so he might shine.
3. O Pavamana, grant us the wealth of the uninvited foe,
 And give us sustenance with offspring.
4. The living Somas purified diffuse exhilarating drink,
 Turned to the vat that drips with mead.
5. Soma flows on wise, endowed with sap and mighty strength,
 Brave Hero who repels the curse.
6. For Indra, Soma! You are cleansed, a feast-companion for the gods:
 Indra, you will gladly win us strength.
7. When he has drunk this draught, Indra smites down resolute foes:
 Yes, he smites them, and will smite them still.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXIVṢoma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09024.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Hitherward, Soma flows, its drops purified,
 while they are washed clean in water.
2. Like a flood, the milk runs to meet it,
 as it comes to Indra, cleansed.
3. O Soma Pavamana, you flow to Indra’s drink,
 captured by men, you are led.
4. Victorious, hailed with joy, O Soma,
 flow to delight men, rulers of mankind.
5. You, Indu, when by stones you run to the filter,
 ready for Indra’s high decree.
6. Flow on, best Vṛtra-slayer, flow meet to be praised,
 pure, purifying, wonderful.
7. Pure, purifying is called the Soma,
 slayer of sinners, dear to gods.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09025.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. GREEN-HUED! As one who gives strength, may the gods drink this draught
For Vāyu and the Maruts.
2. O Flame-like One, sent by song, roaring in your abode,
Enter Vāyu as Law commands.
3. The Ox shines with the Deities, dear Sage in his rightful home,
Foe-slayer, most beloved by the gods.
4. Taking each beautiful form, he goes, desirable, pure,
Thither where the immortals sit.
5. To Indra, Soma flows, the Red, wise song-giver, exceeding wise,
The guest of living men.
6. Flow, best exhilarator, Sage, flow to the filter in a stream
To claim your place among the songs.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXVI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09026.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The sages adorned the powerful horse
With care upon Aditi’s lap.
2. Cows called out to him, abundant with a hundred rivers,
To Indu, who upholds the sky.
3. They sent him, nourisher of many, Wise One, creator of Pavamana,
By wisdom to the sky.
4. With Vivasvan dwelling, they sent him
With both arms, Lord of speech unerring.
5. Him, verdant, dear, many-eyed, the Sisters with stone offerings
Send down to the sieve’s ridges.
6. O Pavamana, Indu, priests urge you on to Indra, you
Who bolster song and cheer him.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXVII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09027.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. This Sage, praised by our hymns, flows to the purifying cloth,
 Sweeping away enemies as he is cleansed.
2. Giving power and bringing light, for Indra and for Vāyu he
 Is poured onto the filtering cloth.
3. Men carry him, Soma, Guide, All-Knowing One, and Heir to the Heavens,
 Spilling into the wooden vats.
4. Indu Pavamana longs for cows and gold, still Conqueror, never vanquished.
5. This Pavamana, sweet draught, falls on the filtering cloth, then
 Rises with Sūrya to the sky.
6. This mighty tawny Steer has flowed to Indra in the heavens,
 Purified, Indu, now victorious.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXVIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09028.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Urged by humans, this powerful horse, Lord of minds, All-knowing,
 Races toward the wool spinner.
2. Through the filter it flows, this Soma for the gods, Distributed,
 Entering all their essences.
3. Radiant there, this immortal God in his abode,
 Slayer of foes, dear to the gods.
4. Guided by the Ten Sisters, Roaring on its path, This Ox
 Charges toward the wooden vats.
5. This Pavamana, swift and strong, All-knowing, Gave vigor to
 The Sun and all his forms of light.
6. When this Soma is purified, It flows mightily and unerring,
 Slayer of sinners, dear to the gods.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXIX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09029.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. With powerful flow, the currents move, toward the Gods he steers.
The singers sing his praises, and wise priests adorn the chariot,
Brought forth as light that deserves to be praised.

2. You win these things easily, Soma, Lord of wealth,
Fill up the ocean that claims our praise.

3. Preserve us from the godless, from the voices of the wicked,
So that we may be free from blame.

4. Win all treasures at once, O Soma, with your stream,
Drive our enemies to one place.

5. Preserve us from the godless, from the voices of the wicked,
So that we may be free from blame.

6. O Indu, as you flow, bring us the wealth of earth and heaven,
And splendid vigor, in your stream.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09030.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Streams of this Powerful One have flowed easily to the strainer’s cloth:
While he is cleansed, he lifts his voice.
2. Indu, urged by pressers to go quickly, bellows out while adorned.
It sends forth a very powerful sound.
3. Pour on us, Soma, with your stream conquering might that many desire,
Accompanied by heroic sons.
4. Hither has Pavamana flowed, Soma has flowed hither in a stream,
To settle in the wooden vats.
5. To waters with the stones they drive you, tawny-hued, most sweet,
O Indu, to be Indra’s drink.
6. For Indra, for the Thunderer press the Soma, very rich in sweetness,
Lovely, inspiring, for strength.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09031.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Soma drops, pure and kind, come forth, bestowing wealth that all can see.
2. O Indu, high above heaven and earth, may you increase our might:
   The master of all strength, may you be.
3. The winds are kind to you, the rivers flow to you,
   Soma, may they multiply your power.
4. Soma, grow great. May vigorous powers gather in you:
   Be in the place of strength.
5. For you, brown-hued! The cows have poured imperishable oil and milk,
   Aloft on the highest height.
6. Friendship, O Indu, we desire with you who bear noble arms,
   With you, O Lord of all that is.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09032.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The Soma drops that shower blessings have flowed to honor our king.
2. Then Trita’s maidens urge the golden ones with stones, Indu for Indra, for his drink.
3. Now like a swan he makes all the company sing each his hymn: He, like a steed, is bathed in milk.
4. O Soma, looking at heaven and earth, you run like a swift deer
Set in the place of sacrifice.
5. The cows sang joyfully to him, just as a woman to her lover
He came to a settled race.
6. Grant us illustrious fame, both to our generous lords and me,
Glory, intelligence, and wealth.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09033.htm
--------------------------------------------------
LIKE waves of waters, skilled in song the juices of the Soma speed
Onward, as buffaloes to woods.
With stream of sacrifice the brown bright drops have flowed with strength in store
Of kine into the wooden vats.
To Indra, Vāyu, Varuṇa, to Viṣṇu, and the Maruts, flow
The drops of Soma juice effused.
Three several words are uttered: kine are flowing, cows who give their milk:
The Tawny-hued go bellowing on.
The young and sacred mothers of the holy rite have uttered praise:
They decorate the Child of Heaven.
From every side, O Soma, for our profit, pour thou forth four seas
Filled full of riches thousandfold.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXIV. Some Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09034.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The Soma juice drops flow onward, driven by this powerful stream.
2. It is poured to Indra, Varuṇa, Vāyu, and the host of Maruts,
To Viṣṇu, the Soma juice flows.
3. With stones they press the Soma, guided by the strong one,
They milk it out with skill.
4. He who must refine Trita, he who will make Indra glad:
The Tawny One adorned with colors.
5. His sons milk him, the dwelling place of sacrifice,
Lovely and dear, the offering.
6. To him, in a single, straight-forward stream,
These songs flow forward, loud-voiced,
He makes the cows low with song.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09035.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Pour forth abundant wealth upon us, O Pavamana, with your stream.
With which you can find us light.
2. O Indu, who sways the sea, shaker of all things, flow on,
Bearing wealth mightily to us.
3. With you as our Hero, Valiant One! May we subdue our enemies:
Let precious things flow to us.
4. Indu, you stir up strength in the Sage who seeks victory, gaining power,
Discovering sacred works and ways.
5. Mover of speech, we clothe him in our songs as he is cleansed
Soma, the protector of the folk;
6. On his path, Lord of Holy Law, as he is cleansed, he is rich.
All people have set their hearts.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXVI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09036.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. From the mortar comes the juice, like a swift horse, to the sieve:
The Steed advances to the finish line.
2. Thus, Soma, vigilant and skilled, cheering the gods, pass through the sieve,
Turned to the vat that yields rich cream.
3. Excellent Pavamana, let the light shine brightly for us.
Grant us mental prowess and skill.
4. You, adorned by devout people, and coming from their hands, flowing through the fine cloth,
Flow through the straining cloth.
5. May Soma pour all the treasures of the sky, the earth, and the firmament
Upon the generous worshipper.
6. You climb to the heights of heaven, O Soma, seeking horses and cattle,
And seeking heroes, Lord of Strength!


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXVII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09037.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Soma, the Cow, poured out for drinking, flows into the purifying sieve,
 Slashing the demons, loved by the gods.
2. Far-seeing, golden-brown, it flows into the sieve, wise,
 Roaring, to its resting place.
3. This vigorous Pavamana rushes to the bright realm of heaven,
 Slayer of foes, through the fleece sieve.
4. This Pavamana, up above Trita’s high peak, made the Sun,
 With the sisters, shine together.
5. This Vṛtra-slaying Cow, poured out, Soma-giver, never cheated,
 Went, as if, to claim the spoils.
6. Driven forward by the sage, the god advances to the wooden casks,
 Indu to Indra willingly.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXVIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09038.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. THIS chariot rushes through the woolen sieve, as it goes
 To battle that wins a thousand prizes.
 2 THE wives of Trita with the stones urge on this Golden One
 Indu to Indra for his drink.
 3 TEN nimble fingers carefully adorn him here; they make him bright
 And beautiful for the joyful drink.
 4 HE like a falcon settles among the clans of men.
 Moving like a lover to his love.
 5 THIS youthful invigorating juice looks downward from its place in heaven,
 This Soma drop that pierced the sieve.
 6 Poured for the drink, this golden juice
 Flows forth, intelligent, crying out,
 To the beloved place.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XXXIX Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09039.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Flow on, O you of noble thoughts, flow swiftly in your beloved form,
Saying, I go where the gods reside.

2. Prepare what has not yet been prepared, and bring food to man,
Make the rain descend from heaven.

3. With might, granting power, the juice passes through the purifying sieve,
Far-sighted, sending out its light.

4. This is it that flows rapidly down from heaven alongside the river’s wave,
From the heavens onto the strained cloth.

5. Inviting him from afar and even close by, the juice
Is poured out for Indra.

6. They have sung the hymn together; with stones they urge the Golden One.
Sit in the place of sacrifice.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XL. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09040.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The very active one has attacked and purified all enemies:
 They adorn the Sage with holy songs.
2. The Red one has ascended to his place; to India, the mighty juice goes:
 He settles in his firm dwelling.
3. O Indu, Soma, send us now great prosperity from every side,
 Pour on us thousands of treasures.
4. O Soma Pavamana, bring all splendor hitherward:
 Give us food in abundance.
5. As you are cleansed, bring heroic strength and wealth to your worshipper,
 And may your hymns prosper.
6. O Indu, Soma, being cleansed, bring here double-piled riches,
 Wealth, mighty Indu, fit for praise.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09041.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Bright and active they have come, swift as bulls, driving dark-skinned foes far.
2. We think on the bridge of joy, leaving the bridge of sorrow behind.
3. The mighty Pavamana roars, like rain, lightning flashes to the sky.
4. Pour out abundant food on us, O Wealth, in cattle, gold, horses, and spoils.
5. May you flow on, Most Active, fill the mighty heavens and earth, as Dawn and Surya do.
6. Flow round us, O Soma, with your protective stream, like Rasa that circles the world.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09042.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. GIVING birth to the Sun in floods, giving birth to heaven’s lights, green-hued,
 Born in the waters and the milk,
 2 According to the ancient plan, this Soma, with his flow, dispenses
 Purely, a God for Gods.
 3 For him victorious, grown great, the juices with a thousand powers
 Are purified for victory’s gain.
 4 Pouring out the ancient fluid, he is filtered through the cleanser:
 He, thundering, has created the Gods.
 5 Soma, as it purifies, sends here everything we desire,
 It sends the Gods who uphold the Law.
 6 Soma, flowing forth, pour on us wealth in cattle, in heroes, horses, and spoils,
 Send us an abundance of food.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09043.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. WE will sing a sacred song for the Lovely One, who rides as a Steed,
 Dressed in milk for rapturous joy.
 2 All our songs seek grace, in the ancient way,
 For Indra, for his drink.
 3 Soma flows freely when it's purified, dear and sung by sages,
 Songs of Medhyātithi.
 4 O Soma Pavamana, grant us exceeding glory,
 Riches, Indu, full of boundless might.
 5 Like a swift steed racing to the prize, loved by the gods,
 Roars as he passes through the sieve.
 6 Flow on your path to give us strength, to make the sage strong:
 Soma, grant heroic power.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLIV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09044.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. INDU, for this great ritual, bring your waves to the Gods,
Unwavering, you flow for us.
2. With the hymn pleased, urged by prayer, Soma hurries far away,
The Wise One in the singer’s stream.
3. Vigilant among the gods, this juice moves toward the cleansing sieve,
Soma, most active, travels on.
4. Flow forward, seeking strength for us, adorning the sacrifice:
The priest calls you with his trimmed grass.
5. May Soma, always bringing power to Bhaga and Vāyu, Sage
And Hero, lead us to the Gods.
6. Thus, to increase our wealth today, Inspirer, best of Furtherers,
Grant us strength and high renown.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09045.htm
--------------------------------------------------
Flow, you who behold men, to grant them pleasure and to please the gods,
Indu, to Indra for his drink.
Stream to your embassy for us; you hasten for Indra to the gods, oh better than our friends.
We anoint you, red in hue, with milk to prepare you for the ecstatic joy;
Open for us the doors of wealth.
He has passed through the sieve, like a swift horse to the pole, to run;
All friends have praised him as he dances in the woods, beyond the fleece.
Singers have sung Indu’s praises.
Flow, Indu, in that stream in which you proclaim to the man
Who worships you, his heroic strength.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLVI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09046.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. LIKE swift horses they have been sent forth to be the feast of gods,
joying in mountains, flowing on.
2. To Vāyu flow the Soma-streams, the drops of juice made beautiful
Like a bride dowered by her sire.
3. Pressed in the mortar, these, the drops of juice, the Somas rich in food,
Give strength to Indra with their work.
4. Deft-handed men, run hither, seize the brilliant juices blended with meal,
And cook with milk the gladdening draught.
5. Thus, Soma, Conqueror of wealth! flow, finding furtherance for us,
Giver of ample opulence.
6. This Pavamana, meet to be adorned, the fingers ten adorn,
The draught that shall make Indra glad.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLVII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09047.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. GREAT as he was, Soma gained strength through this high ceremony:
 Joyfully he rises like a bull.
 2 His task is done: his crushing of the Dasyus is evident:
 He sternly counts their debts.
 3 As soon as his praise-song is born, the Soma, Indra’s nectar, becomes
 A thousand-destroying thunderbolt.
 4 Seer and Sustainer, he himself desires wealth for the wise one
 When he decorates his songs.
 5 They both wish to win wealth as in horse races. In battle
 You stand on the side of the victors.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLVIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09048.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. WITH YAJNA WE SEEK TO YOU KIND CHERISHER OF MANLY MIGHT
 IN THEMSES OF THE HIGH HEAVENS;
 2 GLADDENING CRUSHER OF THE BRAVE, RULED WITH VERY MIGHTY STRENGTH,
 DESTROYER OF A HUNDRED FORTS.
 3 HENCE, WISE ONE! THE FALCON, STRONG OF WING, UNWEARIED, Brought You Down,
 LORD OVER RICHES, FROM THE SKY.
 4 THAT EACH MAY SEE THE LIGHT, THE BIRD BROUGHT US THE GUARD OF LAW, THE FRIEND
 OF ALL, THE SPEEDER THROUGH THE AIR.
 5 AND NOW, SENT FORTH, IT HAS ATTAINED TO MIGHTY POWER AND MAJESTY,
 MOST ACTIVE, READY TO ASSIST.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN XLIX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09049.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Pour down the rain upon us, send a wave of water from the sky,
And fill our land with bountiful crops.
2. Let that stream of yours flow forward, by which the cows came to us,
The cattle of strangers to our home.
3. You are the chief friend of the gods in sacred rites, pour on us richness with your stream,
Pour down upon us a flood of rain.
4. To give us strength, let that stream run through the woolly fleece,
For truly the gods will carry it.
5. Pāvamāna has flowed forward and driven off the Rakṣasas,
Flashing forth brilliance as of old.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN L. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09050.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. YOUR POWER ROARS LIKE A RIVER, STRIKING THROUGH WITH ARROW POINTS:
 Urge on your sharp arrows.
 2 THREE JOYFUL VOICES RISE UPWARD AS YOU FLOW OVER THE FLEECE,
 When you pour forth upon the white wool.
 3 WITH STONE AND TAWNY WELL-BELoved ONE, THEY URGE YOU TO THE SIEVE,
 Even Pavamana, dripping meath.
 4 FLOW TO THE SIEVE, MOST POWERFUL SAGE TO ENJOY,
 To seat yourself in the place of song.
 5 FLOW, MOST EXCITING! ANOINTED WITH MILK FOR BLESSING,
 Indu, for Indra, for his drink.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09051.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. ADHVARYU, pour the Soma juice expressed with stones,
And make it pure for Indra's drink.
2. Pour out for Indra, Thunder-armed, the milk of heaven,
The Soma's juice, most excellent, most rich in sweets.
3. These Gods and all the Maruts, Indu enjoy this juice of thine,
This Pavamana’s flowing mead.
4. For, Soma, you have been poured out, strengthening for the wild feast,
O Steer, the singer, for our help.
5. Flow with your stream, Far-sighted One, poured out, into the cleansing sieve:
Flow on to give us strength and fame.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09052.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. WEALTH-WINNER, in the sky you dwell, bringing us strength with your nectar,
 Pour through the filter as you flow.
2. May he, dear one, in his ancient ways,
 Run over the fine cloth, a thousand times.
3. Shake him, like a caldron, O Indu, shake our gift,
 With your mighty arms, Warrior!
4. Indu, invoked with many prayers, bring down the strength of these men,
 Of him who threatens us with war.
5. Indu, Wealth-giver, with your help pour out for us a hundred, yes,
 A thousand of your pure bright streams.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09053.htm
--------------------------------------------------
O Deva with stones as arms, your might that vanquishes foes has risen:
Drive back our enemies.

With might you strike down those who surround us in battle;
With fearless heart, I'll sing your praise.

None shall assail this holy law with wicked intent;
Crush him who seeks to fight with you.

For Indra drives the tawny horse that drops delight,
Indu, the bringer of joy.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LIV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09054.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. After his ancient radiance, they, the brave, drew the bright nectar from
 The Sage who wins a thousand gifts.
2. He looks like the Sun; he rushes to the lakes,
 Seven streams flowing through the sky.
3. Shining in his glory, he stands above all that exists—
 Soma, like Sūrya, a God.
4. You, Indu, in your brilliance, pour wealth on us,
 As Indra’s friend, from the cows to feed the gods.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09055.htm
--------------------------------------------------
May you fill us with your nectar, all kinds of grain and sustenance,  
O Soma, and all good fortune.  
2 As yours is praise, and what springs from your juice,  
Sit down on this dear sacred grass.  
3 And, giving us cows and horses, O Soma, with your nectar flow  
Through days that pass so swiftly.  
4 As one who conquers, never defeated, attacks and holds back the foe,  
Thus, Vanquisher of many, flow.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LVI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09056.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. QUICKLY the sacred Soma flows through the purifying sieve, as exalted Law,
 Slaying the demons, loved by the gods.
 2 When Soma offers the nourishing food, a hundred active streams
 To win Indra's friendship in his way.
 3 Ten maidens sang to welcome you, as a maiden greets her lover:
 O Soma, you are adorned to win.
 4 Flow hitherward, O Indu, sweet to Indra and to Vishnu: protect
 The men and singers from distress.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LVII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09057.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Thy rivers that never run dry or waste flow out like rain from heaven,
 Bringing thousands of strengths.
2. He flows, beholding all beloved sacred teachings on his path,
 Green-tinted, waving his arms.
3. He, when the people dress him like a docile elephant king,
 Sits as a falcon in the forest.
4. So bring hither to us, Indu, while you are pure,
 All treasures both from heaven and earth.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LVIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09058.htm
--------------------------------------------------
We have accepted thousands from Dhvasra's and Puruṣanti's hands:
Swift runs this giver of delight.
We have accepted thus thousands and three times ten beside:
Swift runs this giver of delight.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LIX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09059.htm
--------------------------------------------------
Flow onward, Soma, with your kine and horses, and all that brings joy:
Bring wealth and offspring here.
Flow from the waters, flow, unbroken, from the plants:
Flow from the pressing boards.
Soma, as Pavamana, pass over all troubles and distress:
Sit on the sacred grass, Sage.
Thou, Pavamana, founded light; at thy birth thou becamest great:
O Indu, thou art over all.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09060.htm
--------------------------------------------------
SING forth and praise with sacred song most active Pavamana, praise
 Indu who sees with thousand eyes.

The one with thousand eyes to see, bearing thousand burdens, they
 Filtered through the woolen cloth.

Pavamana, he has streamed through the cloth; he runs into the jars,
 Finding his way to Indra’s heart.

May Indra be generous, most active Soma, for our well-being:
 Bring good seed with offspring.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LXI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09061.htm
--------------------------------------------------
Flow onward, Indu, with this offering for him who in your wild dance
Battered the ninety-nine and struck,
Smashed forts and gambaras, then Yadu and Turvaga,
For pious Devodasa's sake.

Finder of horses, pour on us horses and wealth in cattle and gold,
And, Indu, food in abundant stores.

We seek your friendly love, even Pavamana’s flowing stream
Beyond the cleansing sieve’s limit.

With those same waves that overflow the purifying sieve,
Soma, be gracious to us.

O Soma, being purified, bring us riches and food with hero sons.
Here, the Child born by streams, adorned by Adityas,
With Indra and Vāyu, effulgent, flows onward with Sūrya’s beams
To the cleansing sieve.

Flow rich in sweetness and lovely for our Bhaga, Vāyu, Pūṣan,
For Mitra and Varuṇa.

High is thy juice’s birth: though set in heaven, on earth it has strong sheltering power and great renown.

Striving to win, with him we gain all wealth from the ungodly man,
Yea, all the glories of mankind.

With Indra and the Maruts, flow for Indra whom we must adore,
For Varuṇa and the Marut host.

The Gods have come well-born, beautified with milk,
The active crusher of the foe.

Even as mother cows strengthen their calves, let our praise-songs
Strengthen him, who wins Indra’s heart.

Pour blessings on our kine, pour forth the milk-rich food,
Increase the sea that merits praise.

From heaven, Pavamana made the marvel thunder, and
All mankind’s lofty light.

The joyous and auspicious juice of thee, Pavamana, King!
Flows over the woolen straining cloth.

Thy juice, O Pavamana, sends its rays like splendid skill,
Like luster, all heaven’s light, to see.

Flow onward with that excellent juice, bringing delight,
Slaying the wicked, dear to gods.

Killing the foe and his hatred, and winning booty every day,
Gainer art thou of steeds and kine.

Red-hued, blend with the milk that seems to yield its lovely breast,
Falcon-like resting in thine home.

Flow onward thou who strengthened Indra to slaughter Vṛtra who
Compassed and stayed the mighty floods.

S


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LXII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09062.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. These swift Soma drops have been filtered through the purifying sieve
To bring us all happiness.
2. Dispelling manifold misfortune, granting the horse’s offspring,
And the warrior’s steed, success.
3. Bringing prosperity to cattle, they cause the perennial Iḷā to flow
For us in noble praise.
4. Strong, born of mountains, the stalk has been pressed
In streams for joyous delight:
Like a hawk settling at home.
5. Fair is the God-beloved juice; the plant is washed in water, pressed by men
The milch-cows sweeten it with milk.
6. As drivers adorn a horse, so they have adorned the meath’s juice for
Ambrosia, for the festival.
7. You, Indu, with your sweet-flowing streams, which were poured for help,
Have settled in the cleansing sieve.
8. So flow you onward through the fleece, for Indra flow, to be his drink,
Finding your home in wooden vats.
9. As giving room and freedom, as most sweet, pour forth butter and milk,
O Indu, for the Aṅgirases.
10. Most active and benevolent, this Pavamana, sent to us
For lofty friendship, meditates.
11. Queller of curses, mighty, with strong sway, this Pavamana shall
Bring treasures to the worshipper.
12. Pour upon us thousands of possessions, both of cattle and steeds,
Exceedingly glorious, much-desired.
13. Wandering far, with wise designs, the juice here present is diffused,
Made beautiful by living men.
14. For Indra flows the gladdening drink, the measurer of the region, Sage,
With countless wealth and endless help.
15. Born on the mountain, praised here, Indu for Indra is set down,
As in her sheltering nest a bird.
16. Pressed by the men, as if to war has Pavamana sped,
To test with might within the vats.
17. That he may move, they yoke him to the three-backed triple-seated car
By the Seven Ṛṣis’ holy songs.
18. Drive that Tawny Courser, O ye pressers, on your way to war,
Swift Steed who carries off the spoil.
19. Pouring all glory here, he stands like a hero among the kine,


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LXIII. Soma Pavanana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09063.htm
--------------------------------------------------
Pour, O Soma, wealth in thousands and heroic strength,
And keep our renown secure.

Thou makes food and vigor swell for Indra, best of gladeners!
Within the cups thou sittest.

For Indra and Viṣṇu, Soma flows into the jar:
May Vāyu find it rich in sweetness.

These swift and brown Soma drops, in the solemn stream of sacrifice,
Flow through twisted obstacles, performing noble deeds.

Driving away the godless ones, Indra's strength augmenting,
Active and augmenting Indra's power.

Brown Soma drops, seeking Indra, flow to their proper place,
Through the region hitherward.

With that stream, give light to Sūrya, urging on waters good to men.
Pavamana, high above man, yokes the Sun's horse Etaśa,
To travel through the realm of air.

Those ten coursers, tawny-hued, harness them so the Sun may come,
Indu, he says, is Indra himself.

Singers, pour the gladdening juice to Vāyu and Indra,
Pour the drops upon the fleece.

O Soma Pavamana, find wealth for us not to be attacked,
Wealth that the foe cannot win.

Send riches hither in thousands, both of steeds and cattle,
Send spoil of war and high renown.

Soma, the God, flowing with stones like Sūrya,
Pour the juice within the jar.

Brilliant drops pour for us, in the solemn sacrifice,
Worshipful laws and strength in cattle.

Over the cleansing sieve, Somas blend with curdled milk,
Effused for Indra, Thunder-armed.

Soma, most sweet in taste, dear to gods, flow to the sieve,
Bring us wealth.

For Indra, living men adorn the Tawny Courser in the streams, Indu, the giver of delight.
Pour for us, Soma, wealth in gold, in horses and heroic sons,
Bring hither strength in herds of cattle.

For battle as it were in war, pour for us, Soma, wealth in herds,
Strength in the flocks of cattle.

Singers, seeking help, adorn the Sage who must be decked with songs:
Loud bellowing the Steer comes on.

The singers with their thoughts and hymns cause Soma, active Steer, to roar.
Gods working with mankind, flow on; to Ind

HYMN LXIV. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09064.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. Soma, you are a splendid Steer, a Steer, O God, with a steely sway:
 You ordain laws like a Steer.
 2. Your strength is like a Steer’s, your wood is strong, you are like a Steer in your drink.
 You are indeed a Steer, O Steer, you are.
 3. You, Indu, as a vigorous horse, have neighed together steeds and kine:
 Open the doors to wealth for us.
 4. From the desire of cows, steeds, and horses, potent Soma drops,
 Bright and swift, have been poured out.
 5. They purify in both hands, made beautiful by holy men,
 Flowing to the fleecy cloth.
 6. These Soma juices will pour forth all treasures for the worshipper
 From heaven and earth and sky.
 7. Your Pavamana streams, Finder of all, have been poured out,
 Just like Sūrya’s rays of light.
 8. Shining from heaven, you flow to every form,
 Soma, you swell like a sea.
 9. Urged on, you send out your voice, O Pavamana;
 You moved, like Sūrya, to the sieve.
 10. Indu, Enlightener, Friend, has been purified by the sages’ hymns:
 So starts the charioteer’s steed.
 11. Your God-delighting wave that flowed to the purifying sieve,
 Alighting in the home of Law.
 12. Flow to our sieve, a joyful draught that intermingles with gods,
 Indu, to Indra for his drink.
 13. Flow onward with a stream for sustenance, made beautiful by wise men:
 Indu, with shine, approach the milk.
 14. While you cleanse, Song-Lover, bring comfort and vigor to the folk,
 Poured, Tawny One! on milk and curds.
 15. Purified for the gods’ feast, go to Indra’s special place,
 Resplendent, guided by the strong.
 16. Accelerated by the hymn, the rapid drops of Soma juice
 Flow, urged onward, to the lake.
 17. Easily have the living drops, made beautiful, approached the lake,
 Yea, to the place of sacrifice.
 18. Circle around, our faithful friend

1. THE, shining maidens send Sūra forth, the glorious sisters, closely allied,
 Send Indu forth, their mighty Lord.
 2 Pervade, O Pavamana, all our treasures with repeated light,
 God, coming hither from the Gods.
 3 Pour on us, Pavamana, rain, as service and rain praise for Gods:
 Pour all to be our nourishment.
 4 Thou art a Steer by luster: we, O Pavamana, faithfully
 Call upon thee the Splendid One.
 5 Do thou, rejoicing, nobly-armed! pour upon us heroic strength:
 O Indu, come thou bitherward.
 6 When thou art cleansed with both the hands and dipped in waters, with the wood.
 Thou comest to the gathering-place.

 The Mighty One with thousand eyes;
 8 Whose colored sap they drive with stones, the yellow meath-distilling juice,
 Indu for Indra, for his drink.
 9 We seek to gain the friendly love of thee that Strong and Mighty One,
 Of thee the winner of all wealth.
 10 Flow onward with thy stream, a Steer, inspiring the Maruts’ Lord,
 Winning all riches by thy might.
 11 I send thee forth to battle from the press, O Pavamana, Strong,
 Sustainer, looker on the light.
 12 Acknowledged by this song of mine, flow, tawny-coloured, with thy stream
 Incite to battle thine ally.
 13 O Indu, visible to all pour out for us abundant food:
 Soma, be thou our prosperer.
 14 The pitchers, Indu, with thy streams have sung aloud in vigorous might
 Enter them, and let Indra drink.
 15 O thou whose potent gladdening juice they milk out with the stones, flow on,
 Destroyer of our enemies.
 16 King Pavamana is implored with holy songs, on man's behalf,
 To travel through the firmament.
 17 Bring us, O Indu, hundredfold increase of kine, and noble steeds,
 The gift of fortune for our help.
 18 Pressed for the banquet of the Gods, O Soma, bring us might, and speed,
 Like beauty for a brilliant show.

HYMN LXVI. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09066.htm
--------------------------------------------------
FOR holy lore of every sort, flow onward thou whom all men love.
A Friend to be besought by friends.

O'er all thou rulest with these Two which, Soma Pavamana, stand,
Turned, as thy stations, hitherward.

Wise Soma Pavamana, thou encompassest on every side
Thy stations as the seasons come.

Flow onward, generating food, for precious boons of every kind,
A Friend for friends, to be our help.

Upon the lofty ridge of heaven thy bright rays with their essences,
Soma, spread purifying power.

O Soma, these Seven Rivers flow, as being thine, to give command:
The Streams of milk run forth to thee.

Flow onward, Soma in a stream, effused to gladden Indra's heart,
Bringing imperishable fame.

Driving thee in Vivasvān's course, the Seven Sisters with their hymns
Made melody round thee the Sage.

The virgins deck thee o’er fresh streams to drive thee to the sieve when thou,
A singer, bathest in the wood.

The streams of Pavamana, thine, Sage, Mighty One, have poured them forth.
Like coursers eager for renown.

They have been poured upon the fleece towards the meath-distilling vat:
The holy songs have sounded forth.

Like milch-kine coming home, the drops of Soma juice have reached the lake,
Have reached the place of sacrifice.

O Indu, to our great delight the running waters flow to us,
When thou wilt robe thyself in milk.

In this thy friendship, and with thee to help us, fain to sacrifice,
Indu, we crave thy friendly love.

Flow on, O Soma, for the great Viewer of men, for gain of Idne
Enter thou into Indra's throat.

Best art thou, Soma, of the great, Strongest of strong ones, Indu: thou
As Warrior ever hast prevailed.

Mightier even than the strong, more valiant even than the brave,
More liberal than the bountiful,

Soma, as Sūra, bring us food, win offspring of our bodies: we
Elect thee for our friendship, we elect thee for companionship.

Agni, thou pourest life; send down upon us food and vigorous strength;
Drive thou misfortune far away.

Agni is Pavamana, Sage, Chief Priest of all the Races Five:

19. Bruised by the press-stones and extolled, Soma, you go to the sieve,
Giving the worshipper hero strength.

--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LXVIII. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09068.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. The drops of Soma juice like cows that yield their milk have flowed forth, rich in meath, to the Shining One,
And, seated on the grass, raising their voice, assumed the milk, the covering robe where the udders stream.

2. He roars with a loud bellow around the highest twigs; the Tawny One is sweetened as he breaks them up.
Then passing through the sieve into the ample room, the God throws off the dregs according to his wish.

3. The gladdening drink that measures out the meeting Twins fills full with milk the Eternal Ever-waxing Pair.
Bringing to light the Two great Regions limitless, moving above them he gains shine that never fades.

4. Wandering through, the Parents, strengthening the floods, the Sage makes his place swell with his own native might.
The stalk is mixed with grain; he comes led by the men together with the sisters, and preserves the Head.

5. With energetic intellect the Sage is born, deposited as germ of Law, far from the Twins.
They being young at first showed visibly distinct the Creature that is half-concealed and half-exposed.

6. The sages knew the form of him the Gladdener, what time the Falcon brought the plant from far away.
He who assures success they beautified in streams, the stalk who yearned therefor, mighty and meet for praise.

7. Together with the Rishis, with their prayers and hymns ten women deck thee, Soma, friendly when effused.
Led by the men, with invocations of the Gods, through the fleece, thou hast given us strength to win the spoil.

8. Songs resonant with praise have celebrated him. Soma, Friend, springing forth with his fair company.
Even him who rich in meath, with undulating stream, Winner of Wealth, Immortal, sends his voice from heaven,

9. He sends it into all the region forth from heaven. Soma, while he is filtered, settles in the jars.
With milk and waters is he decked when pressed with stones: Indu, when purified, shall find sweet rest and room.

10. Even thus poured forth, How on thy way, O Soma, vouchsafing us most manifold lively vigour.
We will invoke benevolent Earth and Heaven. Give us, ye Gods, riches with noble heroes.


--------------------------------------------------
HYMN LXIX. Soma Pavamana.
URL: https://sacred-texts.com/hin/rigveda/rv09069.htm
--------------------------------------------------
1. LIKE AN ARROW ON THE BOW, THE HYMN WAS LOOSE-DOWN, LIKE A YOUNG CALF TO ITS DAM'S UDDER.
As one who comes first with a full stream, she is milked, the Soma is compelled to this man's holy rites.

2. THE THOUGHT IS DEEPLY FIXED; THE SAVOURY JUICE IS SHED; THE TONGUE WITH JOYOUS SOUND IS STIRRING IN THE MOUTH.
And Pavamana, like the shout of combatants, the drop rising in sweet juice, is flowing through the fleece.

3. HE FLOWS ABOUT THE SHEEP-SKIN, LONGING FOR A BRIDE; HE LOOSES ADITI'S DAUGHTERS FOR THE WORSHIPPER.
The sacred drink has come, gold-tinted, well-restrained; like a strong bull, he shines, whetting his manly might.

4. THE BULL IS BELLOWING; THE COWS ARE COMING NIGH; THE GODS APPROACH THE GOD'S OWN RESTING-PLACE.
Onward has Soma passed through the sheep's fair bright fleece, and has, as if, endowed a newly washed garment.

5. GOLD-HUED, IMMORTAL, NEWLY BATHED, PUTS ON A BRIGHTLY SHINING VESTURE THAT IS NEVER HARMED.
He made the ridge of heaven to be his radiant robe, by sprinkling of the bowls from moisture of the sky.

6. EVEN AS THE BEAMS OF SURYA, URGING MEN TO SPEED, THAT CHEER AND SEND TO SLEEP, TOGETHER THEY RUSH OUT.
These swift outpourings in long courses of holy rites: no form save only Indra shows itself so pure.

7. AS DOWN THE STEEP SLOPE OF A RIVER TO THE VALE, DRAWN FROM THE STEER THE SWIFT STRONG DRAUGHTS HAVE FOUND A WAY.
Well be it with the men and cattle in our home. May powers, O Soma, may the people stay with us.

8. POUR OUT UPON US WEALTH IN GOODS, IN GOLD, IN STEEDS, IN CATTLE AND IN CORN, AND GREAT HEROIC STRENGTH.
Ye, Soma, are my fathers, lifted up on high as heads of heaven and makers of the strength of life.

9. THESE PAVAMANAS HERE
